/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetPrayerTime]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetPrayerTime](      
    @PrayerId as int  
)  
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)  
AS  
BEGIN  
declare @result varchar(20)      
select @result=case @PrayerId
when 1 then 'Fajr'
when 2 then 'Before Dhuhr'
when 3 then 'Dhuhr/Juma''ah'
when 4 then 'Asr'
when 5 then 'Maghrib'
when 6 then 'Isha''a'
when 7 then 'After Isha''a'
else ''
end 
return @result   
end
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Payment](

	[PaymentLocation] [int] NULL,
	[OfficerId] [int] NULL,
	[ReceiptNo] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[ExtraAmountCharge] [money] NULL,
	[ExtraAmountReason] [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	[ExtraAmountReceipt] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[PaymentStatus] [tinyint] NULL,
	[EasyPaisaTranNo] [nchar](30) NULL,
	[CreatedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[ModifiedBy] [int] NOT NULL,

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveNearestCentre]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveNearestCentre] 
@Id	int,
@CentreId	int,
@NearestCentreId	int,
@IsActive	bit,
@CreatedBy	int,
@ModifiedBy	int,
@ModifiedDate	datetime

AS
BEGIN	
	if @Id is not null and @Id > 0
	begin
	update [NearestAlkhidmatCentre] with(rowlock)
	set 
	CentreId =  @CentreId,NearestCentreId = @NearestCentreId,IsActive = @IsActive,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate
	where id = @Id
	select * from [NearestAlkhidmatCentre] (nolock) where Id = @Id
	end	
	else
	begin
	insert into [NearestAlkhidmatCentre] with(rowlock)
	(CentreId,NearestCentreId,IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)
	values
	(@CentreId,@NearestCentreId,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)
	select * from [NearestAlkhidmatCentre] (nolock) where Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()
	end
	
END
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[UnionCouncil](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[TownId] [int] NULL,
	[Name] [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	[IsActive] [bit] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_GetBoolean]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetBoolean](                  
    @Id as bit
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(5)          
AS          
begin  
declare @result varchar(50)              
  
if @Id=1
begin
	set @result='Yes'
end
else
begin
	set @result='No'
end
return @result

   
end

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_GetParyer]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetParyer](                  
    @Id as int  
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(500)          
AS          
begin  
declare @result varchar(max)              
  
select @result = case when @id = 1 then 'Fajr' 
when @Id=2 then 'Before Dhuhr'
when @Id=3 then 'Dhuhr/Juma''ah'
when @Id=4 then 'Asr'
when @Id=5 then 'Maghrib'
when @Id=6 then 'Isha''a'
when @Id=7 then 'After Isha''a' end
return @result   
end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_GetGender]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetGender](                
    @Id as int
    )        
RETURNS VARCHAR(500)        
AS        
begin
declare @result varchar(max)            

select @result = case when @Id=1 then 'Male'
	when @Id=2 then 'Female' 
	else null
	end
return @result 
end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_PaymentStatus]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_PaymentStatus](                  
    @Id as int  
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(500)          
AS          
begin  
declare @result varchar(max)              
  
select @result = case when @Id= 1 then 'UnPaid'
when @Id= 2 then 'Paid'
when @Id= 3 then 'Refund'
end
--u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName  from [User] u where id = @Id
return @result   
end
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Landmark](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[UcId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[Name] [nvarchar](100) NOT NULL,
	[IsActive] [bit] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[ModifiedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[ModifiedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Landmark] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[Id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Graveyard](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[LandmarkId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[Name] [varchar](100) NOT NULL,
	[IsActive] [bit] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CreatedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	[ModifiedBy] [int] NOT NULL,
	[ModifiedDate] [datetime] NOT NULL,

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetBusStatus]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  FUNCTION [dbo].[GetBusStatus](      
    @BusStatus as int  
)  
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)  
AS  
BEGIN  
declare @result varchar(20)      
select @result=case @BusStatus 
when 1 then 'Available'
when 2 then 'Booked - Unpaid'
when 3 then 'Booked - Paid'
when 4 then 'Available Soon'
when 5 then 'Maintenance'
when 6 then 'Puncher'
when 7 then 'Unavailable'
else 'Available'
end 
--from Bus where id=@BusId

return @result   
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetNearestCentreByCriteria]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetNearestCentreByCriteria]    
@Id int    
as    
begin    
select bv.Id, bv.BookingId,bv.OutTime,bk.Address,l.Name as BusPoint,g.Name as Graveyard,bk.MasjidName,[dbo].[GetPrayerTime](bk.NamazEJanazaHeldIn) as NamazEJanazaHeldIn,bk.NamazEJanazaLocation,bk.OtherDetail,bk.PickupDate
,ts1.Description as PickupTime,ts2.Description as ReturnTime     
,b.VehicleNo,c.Name as CentreName,c.Address CenreAddress,c.ContactNo1,c.ContactNo2,(d.FirstName + ' ' + d.LastName) as fullName,d.Mobile as MobileNo,  
bv.IsActive,bv.CreatedBy,bv.CreatedDate,bv.ModifiedBy,bv.ModifiedDate  
from BusVisit bv (nolock)    
inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=bv.DriverId and bv.BusId=@Id 
and VisitTypeId=2 and IsBookingCompleted=0 AND isnull(BookingId,0)<>0    
inner join Booking bk (nolock) on bk.Id=bv.BookingId    
inner join Landmark l (nolock) on l.Id=bk.BusPoint    
inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId    
inner join Graveyard g (nolock) on g.Id=bk.GraveyardId    
inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.Id=bv.CentreId    
inner join TimeSlot ts1 (nolock) on ts1.Id=bk.PickupTime
inner join TimeSlot ts2 (nolock) on ts2.Id=bk.ReturnTime
    
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetLandmarkById]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetLandmarkById]
@Id int
as
begin
select l.*, u.Name UcDesc 
from [Landmark] l (nolock)
inner join UnionCouncil u (nolock)  on l.UcId =  u.Id
where l.Id =  @Id
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetLandmarkByCriteria]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetLandmarkByCriteria]
@UcId int,
@Name nvarchar(100)
as
begin
select l.*, u.Name UcDesc 
from [Landmark] l (nolock)
inner join UnionCouncil u (nolock)  on l.UcId =  u.Id
where l.UcId =  @UcId and l.Name = @Name
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetGraveyardById]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetGraveyardById]
@Id int
as
begin
select g.* ,  l.Name LandmarkDesc 
from [Graveyard] g (nolock)
inner join Landmark l (nolock) on g.LandmarkId =  l.Id  
where g.Id =  @Id
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetGraveyardByCriteria]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetGraveyardByCriteria]
@LandMarkId int,
@Name nvarchar(100)
as
begin
select g.* ,  l.Name LandmarkDesc 
from [Graveyard] g (nolock)
inner join Landmark l (nolock) on g.LandmarkId =  l.Id  
where g.LandmarkId =  @LandMarkId and g.Name = @Name
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetExtraChargesByBookingId]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetExtraChargesByBookingId]  
@BookingId int  
as  

select isnull(es.Id,0) Id,es.ExtraAmountCharge,es.ExtraAmountReason,es.ExtraAmountReceipt,isnull(es.IsActive,b.isActive) isActive,
isnull(es.CreatedBy,b.CreatedBy) as CreatedBy,isnull(es.CreatedDate,b.CreatedDate) as CreatedDate,isnull(es.ModifiedBy,b.ModifiedBy) as ModifiedBy,
isnull(es.ModifiedDate,b.ModifiedDate) as ModifiedDate, bv.BusId,b.Id as BookingId,bv.FuelAmount as BookingAmount 
from Booking b  (nolock)
inner join BusVisit bv (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BookingId
left join ExtraCharges es (nolock) on es.BookingId=b.Id and es.BusId=bv.BusId
where b.Id=@BookingId
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetCsvBuses]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetCsvBuses](    
    @CentreId AS INT    
)    
RETURNS VARCHAR(MAX)    
AS    
BEGIN    
declare @result varchar(max)        
--select @result = isnull(@result+'  |  ','')+ ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar,bv.IsBookingCompleted),'1') + ' ' + ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar, bv.BusId),'') + ' ' + b.VehicleNo     
--select @result = isnull(@result+'  |  ','')+ ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar,bv.IsBookingCompleted),'1') + ' ' + b.VehicleNo     
--from Bus b     
--left outer join BusVisit bv on b.id=bv.busId and bv.IsBookingCompleted=0 and bv.VisitTypeId=2    
--where b.CentreId=@CentreId    

select @result = isnull(@result+'  |  ','')+ ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar,IsBookingCompleted),'1') + ' ' + ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar, BusId),'') + ' ' + VehicleNo
from(
select distinct b.VehicleNo,ISNULL(bv.IsBookingCompleted,1) as IsBookingCompleted,bv.BusId
--select distinct @result = isnull(@result+'  |  ','')+ ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar,bv.IsBookingCompleted),'1') + ' ' + b.VehicleNo     
from Bus b  (nolock)   
left outer join BusVisit bv (nolock) on b.id=bv.busId 
and bv.IsBookingCompleted=0 and bv.VisitTypeId=2   
where bv.CentreId=@CentreId
) o

return @result     
end
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetAdminBusMilageReport]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAdminBusMilageReport]       
 @FromVisitDate datetime,      
 @ToVisitDate datetime      
AS      
BEGIN      
     
 select ac.Name CentreDesc,bb.Id BusId, bb.VehicleNo , sum(bv.FinalReading -  bv.InitialReading) TotalMilage, count(bv.Id) TotalVisits      
from Bus bb  (nolock)     
inner join BusVisit bv (nolock) on bb.Id =  bv.BusId       
inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on bv.CentreId =  ac.Id      
left join  Booking b (nolock) on b.Id = bv.BookingId       
where DATEDIFF(day,bv.VisitDate, @FromVisitDate) <= 0 and DATEDIFF(DAY, @ToVisitDate ,  bv.VisitDate) <= 0      
group by ac.Name, bb.Id, bb.VehicleNo  
order by ac.Name      
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetAdminBookingReport]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAdminBookingReport]
 @FromBookingDate datetime,
 @ToBookingDate datetime
AS
BEGIN
 --Paid AMount


select a.Centre as Alkhidmatentre , isnull(a.UnpaidAmount, 0) UnpaidAmount, isnull(a.PaidAmount,0) PaidAmount,
isnull(b.[PaidBooking],0) PaidBooking , ISNULL(b.[UnpaidBooking],0)UnpaidBooking from
(
select * from 
(select ac.Name Centre ,  isnull(p.Amount,0) + isnull(p.ExtraAmountCharge,0) As Amount , -- b.id   BookingId,
case when isnull(p.PaymentStatus, 0) =0  then 'UnpaidAmount'
     else 'PaidAmount' end PaymentStatus
from Booking b (nolock)
inner join Payment p (nolock) on b.Id =  p.BookingId 
left join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on p.PaymentLocation =  ac.Id
where DATEDIFF(day,b.PickupDate, @FromBookingDate) <= 0 and DATEDIFF(DAY, @ToBookingDate ,  b.PickupDate) <= 0  
) query
PIVOT(
   SUM(Amount)
      FOR PaymentStatus 
      IN ([UnpaidAmount],[PaidAmount])     
      ) AS PVTTable
) a  
  inner join  
 -- Paid / unpaid Booking  
(
select *  from 
(select ac.Name Centre  ,  b.id   BookingId,
case when isnull(p.PaymentStatus, 0) =0  then 'UnpaidBooking'
     else 'PaidBooking' end PaymentStatus
from Booking b (nolock)
inner join Payment p (nolock) on b.Id =  p.BookingId 
left join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on p.PaymentLocation =  ac.Id
where DATEDIFF(day,b.PickupDate, @FromBookingDate) <= 0 and DATEDIFF(DAY, @ToBookingDate ,  b.PickupDate) <= 0   
) query
PIVOT(
   count(BookingId)
      FOR PaymentStatus 
      IN ([UnpaidBooking],[PaidBooking])     
      ) AS PVTTable 
   )b
   on a.centre=b.Centre
   
END
GO

GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetBusByCriteria]  
@VehicleNo nvarchar(50)  ,
@BookingId int
as  
begin  
if @VehicleNo='-1'
begin
	select b.*,c.Name as CentreDesc 
	from BusVisit bv (nolock)
	inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId
	inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=b.centreid  
	where bv.BookingId=@bookingId
end
else 
begin
	select b.*,c.name as CentreDesc 
	from [Bus] b   (nolock)
	 inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=b.centreid  
	  where b.VehicleNo  =  @VehicleNo and b.IsActive = 1  
end	  
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetBusAvailabilityByBookingId]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[GetBusAvailabilityByBookingId]    
@BookingId int      
as      
declare @NamazEJanazaHeldIn tinyint      
declare @PickupDate  datetime      
--set @BookingId=65      
      
select @NamazEJanazaHeldIn=NamazEJanazaHeldIn,@PickupDate=PickupDate from Booking(nolock) where id=@BookingId      
      
select id,(ob.vehicleno + ' ( ' +CONVERT(varchar,isnull(AlkhidmatBusNo,0)) + ' )')  as Description ,TrackingDeviceId,ob.CentreId,IsActive,CreatedBy,CreatedDate,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate,ISNULL(IsOnMaintainance,0) AS IsOnMaintainance from Bus(nolock) ob     
where id not in      
(      
select Bus.ID      
from Bus(nolock)       
inner join BusVisit bv(nolock) on bv.BusId=bus.Id      
inner join booking b(nolock) on b.Id=bv.BookingId      
where b.NamazEJanazaHeldIn=@NamazEJanazaHeldIn and b.PickupDate=@PickupDate and bv.IsBookingCompleted=0      
)      
union      
select bus.Id,      
case isnull(p.PaymentType,0)       
when 1 then (Bus.vehicleno + ' ( ' +CONVERT(varchar,isnull(AlkhidmatBusNo,0)) + ' )' + ' - Booked - Paid')      
when 2 then (Bus.vehicleno + ' ( ' +CONVERT(varchar,isnull(AlkhidmatBusNo,0)) + ' )' + ' - Booked - Unpaid')      
else (Bus.vehicleno + ' ( ' +CONVERT(varchar,isnull(AlkhidmatBusNo,0)) + ' )' + ' - Available')      
end  as Description ,      
TrackingDeviceId,bus.CentreId ,Bus.IsActive,Bus.CreatedBy,Bus.CreatedDate,Bus.ModifiedBy,Bus.ModifiedDate,ISNULL(IsOnMaintainance,0) AS IsOnMaintainance     
from Bus(nolock)       
inner join BusVisit bv (nolock)on bv.BusId=bus.Id      
inner join booking b(nolock) on b.Id=bv.BookingId      
left join Payment p(nolock) on p.BookingId=b.Id      
where b.NamazEJanazaHeldIn=@NamazEJanazaHeldIn and b.PickupDate=@PickupDate  and bv.IsBookingCompleted=0
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetBusAvailability]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetBusAvailability](      
    @BusId as int,
    @NamazEJanazaHeldIn tinyint,
    @PickupDate datetime
)  
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)  
AS  
BEGIN  
declare @result tinyint

select  @result=COUNT(bv.Id) from BusVisit bv (nolock)
inner join Booking b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BookingId 
where bv.BusId=@BusId and b.NamazEJanazaHeldIn=@NamazEJanazaHeldIn and b.PickupDate=@PickupDate

return @result   
end
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetRefundBookingById]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetRefundBookingById]     
@Id int    
as    
begin    
select bus.Id as busId,bus.Description as busDesc, isnull(rb.Id,0) Id ,  b.Id as BookingId , isnull(rb.RefundAmount, 0) RefundAmount ,      
isnull(rb.RefundOfficeLocation,0)as RefundOfficeLocation , isnull(rb.RefundReason,'')as RefundReason ,     
isnull(rb.RefundReceipt,'') RefundReceipt, isnull(rb.RefundTypeId, 0) as RefundTypeId ,     
ISNULL(rb.ActualBookingAmount ,  bv.FuelAmount) as ActualBookingAmount,    
   isnull(rb.ActualBookingAmount,0) - ISNULL(rb.RefundAmount,0) as AmountDeducted , isnull(rb.RefundOfficer ,  0) RefundOfficer,    
   ISNULL(rb.IsActive ,  b.isactive) as IsActive,    
   ISNULL(rb.CreatedBy ,  b.CreatedBy) as CreatedBy, ISNULL(rb.CreatedDate ,b.CreatedDate) CreatedDate,    
   ISNULL(rb.ModifiedBy , b.ModifiedBy) ModifiedBy, ISNULL(rb.ModifiedDate, b.ModifiedDate) ModifiedDate    
   from Booking b (nolock)    
   inner join BusVisit bv (nolock) on bv.BookingId=b.Id  
   inner join Bus (nolock) on bus.Id=bv.BusId  
--left join Payment p (nolock)  on b.Id =  p.BookingId    
left join RefundBooking rb (nolock)  on b.Id = rb.BookingId  and rb.BusId=bus.Id  
    
where b.Id =  @Id    
  
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetRefundBookingByCriteria]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

where r.BookingId =  @BookingId and r.RefundOfficeLocation = @RefundOfficeLocation
and r.RefundTypeId = @RefundTypeId
end

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetBookingByCriteria]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetBookingByCriteria]        
@ContactInfo varchar(200)=null,        
@DeseasedInfo varchar(200)=null,        
@GenderId smallint=0,        
@PaymentStatusId smallint=-1,        
--@BookingDate datetime,        
@GreveyardId smallint=0,        
@CentreId smallint=0,        
@BusId smallint=0        
as        
begin        
        
select b.*,bv.BusId,bv.CentreId,p.PaymentStatus as status 
from Booking b  (nolock)     
left join Payment p (nolock) on p.BookingId=b.Id      
left join BusVisit bv (nolock) on bv.BookingId=b.Id      
where 1=1      
 -- and ( case when isnull(@ContactInfo,'')<>'' then (b.ContactName like @ContactInfo or b.ContactMobile like @ContactInfo or b.ContactNic like @ContactInfo) end)      
--and case when ISNULL(@DeseasedInfo,'')<>'' then (b.DeseasedName like @DeseasedInfo or b.Address like @DeseasedInfo) end      
and ISNULL(b.ContactName,'%%') like case when ISNULL(@ContactInfo,'')<>'' then @ContactInfo else b.ContactName end      
and isnull(b.DeseasedName,'%%') like case when ISNULL(@DeseasedInfo,'')<>'' then @DeseasedInfo else b.DeseasedName end      
and b.GraveyardId =  case when @GreveyardId<>0 then @GreveyardId ELSE b.GraveyardId end      
and p.PaymentStatus = case when @PaymentStatusId<>-1 then @PaymentStatusId else p.PaymentStatus end      
and b.DeseasedGender= case when @GenderId<>0 then @GenderId else  b.DeseasedGender end      
--and bv.CentreId= case when ISNULL(@CentreId,0)<>0 then @CentreId else bv.CentreId end      
--and p.PaymentLocation = case when ISNULL(@CentreId,'')<>'' then @CentreId else p.PaymentLocation end      
and bv.BusId= case when ISNULL(@BusId,0)<>0 then @BusId else bv.BusId end      
      
end
GO

CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetAllNearestCentreSetup]     
as        
begin        
select nc.Id,ac.Id as CentreId,ac.Name as centreName, ncc.Id NearestCentreId, ncc.Name NearestCentreName, nc.NearestLevel,
nc.CreatedBy, nc.CreatedDate, nc.ModifiedBy, nc.ModifiedDate, nc.IsActive
from NearestCentre nc (nolock)      
inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on ac.Id=nc.CentreId      
inner join AlkhidmatCentre ncc (nolock) on ncc.Id =  nc.NearestCentreId
order by ac.Name, nc.NearestLevel     
end
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ChangeUserPassword]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ChangeUserPassword]
@UserName nvarchar(50),
@Password nvarchar(50) ,
@ResetPassword nvarchar(50)
	
AS
BEGIN
	
	if EXISTS  (select id from [User] (nolock) where username = @username and [password] = @Password)
	begin	
         update [user] with(rowlock) set [Password] =  @ResetPassword where username = @username
	end
	else
	begin
		RAISERROR ('You have entered your wrong current Paasword. Please enter correct current password to reset.', -- Message text.  
         16, -- Severity.  
         1 -- State.   
         );  
	end
	 
END
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[CCTracking_View]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[CCTracking_View]
AS
SELECT     b.Id AS BookingId, b.ContactName, b.ContactMobile, b.ContactNic, b.DeseasedName, b.DeseasedAge, b.DeseasedGender, b.Address AS BookingAddress, 
                      b.BusPoint AS BusPointId, bp.Name AS BusPoint, b.CauseOfDeath AS CauseOfDeathId, cod.Name AS CauseOfDeath, b.LandmarkId, l.Name AS LandMark, b.TownId, 
                      t.Name AS BookingTown, b.GraveyardId, g.Name AS Graveyard, b.PickupDate, b.PickupTime, b.ReturnTime, b.NamazEJanazaHeldIn, b.NamazEJanazaLocation, 
                      b.MasjidName, b.OtherDetail, b.IsActive AS BookingActive, p.Pricing, p.Amount, p.PaymentType AS PaymentTypeId, pt.Name AS PaymentType, p.PaymentStatus, 
                      ac.Name AS BookingCentre, ac.Address AS BookingCentreAddress, ac.ContactNo1 AS BookingCenterContactNo1, ac.ContactNo2 AS BookingCentreContactNo2, 
                      p.OfficerId AS PaymentOfficer, u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName AS PaymentOfficerName, u.Address AS PaymentOfficerAddress, u.CNIC AS PaymentOfficerCnic, 
                      u.CentreId AS PaymentOfficerCentreId, ac2.Name AS PaymentOfficerCentre, p.ReceiptNo, p.ExtraAmountCharge, p.ExtraAmountReason, p.ExtraAmountReceipt, 
                      p.EasyPaisaTranNo, b.CreatedBy AS BookingUser, u2.FirstName + ' ' + u2.LastName AS BookingCreatedBy, b.CreatedDate AS BookingCreatedDate
FROM         dbo.Booking AS b (nolock) LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.CauseOfDeath AS cod (nolock) ON b.CauseOfDeath = cod.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Landmark AS bp (nolock) ON b.BusPoint = bp.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Landmark AS l (nolock) ON b.LandmarkId = l.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Town AS t (nolock) ON b.TownId = t.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Graveyard AS g (nolock) ON b.GraveyardId = g.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Payment AS p (nolock) ON b.Id = p.BookingId LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.PaymentType AS pt (nolock) ON p.PaymentType = pt.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.AlkhidmatCentre AS ac (nolock) ON p.PaymentLocation = ac.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.[User] AS u (nolock) ON p.OfficerId = u.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.AlkhidmatCentre AS ac2 (nolock) ON u.CentreId = ac2.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.[User] AS u2 (nolock) ON b.CreatedBy = u2.Id
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[AdminSummary_View]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE view [dbo].[AdminSummary_View]                
as                         
               
select bk.ContactName, d.FirstName + ' ' + d.LastName as driver,c.Name as centre,cb.name as BookingCentre, (b.VehicleNo + ' (' + cast( isnull( b.AlkhidmatBusNo, '') as varchar(5)) +')') as VehicleNo,bv.BookingId,VisitDate,                
CONVERT(varchar, DATEDIFF(MI,CONVERT(varchar(8),bv.visitDate,1) + ' ' + ts1.description,              
CONVERT(varchar(8),bv.visitDate,1) + ' ' + ts2.description)/60) + ':' + CONVERT(varchar, DATEDIFF(MI,CONVERT(varchar(8),bv.visitDate,1) + ' ' + ts1.description,CONVERT              
(varchar(8),bv.visitDate,1) + ' ' + ts2.description)%60) as visitInterval,                
ts1.description as outTime,ts2.description as returnTime  ,              
isnull(bv.InitialReading, b.initialReading) InitialReading, bv.FinalReading, bv.ReadingWhenFilling as FuelStationReading              
,(bv.FinalReading - bv.InitialReading) as milage,                
bv.InchargeName,               
case when bv.VisitTypeId = 2 then ISNULL( bv.FuelAmount,0) + ISNULL( ec.ExtraAmountCharge,0) -  isnull( rb.RefundAmount,0)  else isnull(bv.FuelAmount,0) end FuelAmount,              
bv.FuelRate, bv.FuelQuantity, bv.PumpLocation,bv.Receipt FuelingReceipt,          
bv.VisitTypeId                
,bv.DriverId,bv.BusId, bv.CentreId,bv.Id as busVisitId  , VT.Name AS VisitType ,            
bk.IsReferralBooking , bk.ReferralName, p.IsReferralBookingPaid, p.ReferralPaymentDate,             
p.ReceiptNo as BookingReceipt,bk.PickupDate  
--,(u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName) as UserName    
from BusVisit bv (nolock) inner join timeslot ts1 on bv.OutTime=ts1.id                
inner join timeslot ts2 (nolock) on bv.ReturnTime=ts2.id                
inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=bv.DriverId                
inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId                
inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.Id=bv.CentreId                
inner join VisitType VT (nolock) on bv.VisitTypeId =  VT.Id      
--inner join [User] u (nolock) on u.Id=bv.ModifiedBy    
left join Booking bk (nolock) on bv.BookingId = bk.Id 
left join AlkhidmatCentre cb (nolock) on cb.Id=bk.alkhidmatCentre               
left join Payment p (nolock) on bv.BookingId = p.BookingId               
left join RefundBooking rb (nolock) on bv.BookingId =  rb.BookingId  and bv.BusId =  rb.BusId            
left join ExtraCharges ec (nolock) on bv.BookingId =  ec.BookingId and bv.BusId =  ec.BusId
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveUser]  
  @Id int,  
 @CentreId int,  
 @RoleId int,  
 @UserName nvarchar(50),  
 @Password nvarchar(100) = null,  
 @FirstName nvarchar(50),  
 @LastName nvarchar(50),  
 @CNIC nvarchar(13)=null,  
 @Mobile nvarchar(13)=null,  
 @Email nvarchar(100)= null,  
 @Address nvarchar(200)=null,  
 @City nvarchar(50)=null,  
 @FromDate datetime =  null,  
 @ToDate datetime =  null,  
 @IsActive bit,  
 @CreatedBy int,  
 @ModifiedBy int ,  
 @ModifiedDate Datetime  
 AS  
 BEGIN  
    
  if @Id is not null and @Id > 0  
  begin  
   update [user]  with(rowlock)
   set   
   CentreId = @CentreId,RoleId=@RoleId,FirstName = @FirstName,LastName = @LastName,CNIC = @CNIC,Mobile = @Mobile,Email = @Email,[Address] = @Address,City = @City,FromDate = @FromDate,ToDate = @ToDate,IsActive = @IsActive,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy ,  ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate  
   where Id = @Id  
    
   select u.*,  ac.Name as CenterDesc, r.Name as RoleDesc   
   from [User] u   (nolock)
   inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on u.CentreId =  ac.Id  
   inner join [Role] r (nolock) on u.RoleId =  r.Id  where u.id=@Id   
  end   
  else  
   begin   
    begin try  
      
    insert into [user]  with(rowlock)
    (CentreId,RoleId,UserName,[Password],FirstName,LastName,CNIC,Mobile,Email,[Address],City,FromDate,ToDate,IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy)  
    values   
    (@CentreId,@RoleId,@UserName,@Password,@FirstName,@LastName,@CNIC,@Mobile,@Email,@Address,@City,@FromDate,@ToDate,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy)  
      
    select @Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()  
      
    select u.*,  ac.Name as CenterDesc, r.Name as RoleDesc   
    from [User] u   (nolock)
    inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on u.CentreId =  ac.Id  
    inner join [Role] r (nolock) on u.RoleId =  r.Id  where u.Id =  @Id  
      
    end try  
    begin catch  
      
    DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
    DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
    DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
    SELECT   
     @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
     @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
     @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
          
    -- Use RAISERROR inside the CATCH block to return error  
    -- information about the original error that caused  
    -- execution to jump to the CATCH block.  
    RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
         @ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
         @ErrorState -- State.   
         );  
                 
    end catch;  
   end   
 END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveRefundBooking]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveRefundBooking]       
@Id int,      
@BusId int,
@BookingId int,      
@RefundTypeId int,      
@RefundReason nvarchar(500),      
@ActualBookingAmount money,      
@RefundAmount money,      
@RefundReceipt nvarchar(50),      
@RefundOfficeLocation int,      
@RefundOfficer int,      
@IsActive bit,      
@CreatedBy int,      
@ModifiedBy int,      
@ModifiedDate datetime      
       
AS      
      
BEGIN      
declare @newId int    
 if exists(select id from refundBooking (nolock) where id=@Id and busId=@BusId)   
 --if @Id is not null and @Id > 0      
 begin      
 set @newId=@Id    
 update [RefundBooking]  with(rowlock)     
 set       
 BusId=@BusId,
 BookingId =  @BookingId,RefundTypeId= @RefundTypeId,RefundReason = @RefundReason,      
 ActualBookingAmount = @ActualBookingAmount,RefundAmount = @RefundAmount,RefundReceipt=@RefundReceipt,       
 RefundOfficeLocation = @RefundOfficeLocation, RefundOfficer = @RefundOfficer,      
 IsActive = @IsActive,CreatedBy = @CreatedBy,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate      
 where id = @newId and busId=@BusId     
    
 end       
 else      
 begin      
     
   
 insert into RefundBooking  with(rowlock)     
 (BusId,BookingId,ActualBookingAmount,RefundOfficeLocation,RefundTypeId,RefundAmount,RefundReason, RefundOfficer,RefundReceipt, IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)      
 values      
 (@BusId,@BookingId,@ActualBookingAmount,@RefundOfficeLocation,@RefundTypeId,@RefundAmount,@RefundReason,@RefundOfficer,@RefundReceipt,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)           
 set @newId=SCOPE_IDENTITY()     
    
 end      
    
 update Payment with(rowlock) set PaymentStatus=2 where BookingId=@BookingId    
 update BusVisit with(rowlock) set IsBookingCompleted=1 where BookingId=@BookingId    
       
 select isnull(rb.Id,0) Id ,rb.BusId,  b.Id as BookingId , isnull(rb.RefundAmount, 0) RefundAmount ,        
 isnull(rb.RefundOfficeLocation,0)as RefundOfficeLocation , isnull(rb.RefundReason,'')as RefundReason ,       
 isnull(rb.RefundReceipt,'') RefundReceipt, isnull(rb.RefundTypeId, 0) as RefundTypeId ,       
 ISNULL(rb.ActualBookingAmount ,  p.Amount) as ActualBookingAmount, isnull(rb.RefundOfficer ,  0) as RefundOfficer,      
 isnull(rb.ActualBookingAmount,0) - ISNULL(rb.RefundAmount,0) as AmountDeducted , ISNULL(rb.IsActive ,  b.isactive) as IsActive,      
 ISNULL(rb.CreatedBy ,  b.CreatedBy) as CreatedBy, ISNULL(rb.CreatedDate ,b.CreatedDate) CreatedDate,      
 ISNULL(rb.ModifiedBy , b.ModifiedBy) ModifiedBy, ISNULL(rb.ModifiedDate, b.ModifiedDate) ModifiedDate      
 from Booking b (nolock)      
 left join Payment p (nolock)  on b.Id =  p.BookingId      
 left join RefundBooking rb (nolock)  on b.Id = rb.BookingId      
 where rb.Id = @newId      
          
END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SavePayment]              
@Id int,           
@BookingId int,          
@PaymentType tinyint ,          
--@Pricing tinyint ,          
@Amount money,          
@PaymentLocation int,          
@OfficerId int ,          
@ReceiptNo nvarchar(100),          
--@ExtraAmountCharge money=null,            
--@ExtraAmountReason nvarchar(1000)=null,          
--@ExtraAmountReceipt nvarchar(100)=null,          
@PaymentStatus tinyint,          
@EasyPaisaTranNo nvarchar(30)=null,      
@IsReferralBookingPaid bit= null,    
@ReferralPaymentDate datetime=null,      
@CreatedBy int,          
@ModifiedBy int,    
@ModifiedDate datetime          
as              
          
IF @Id=null or @Id=0          
BEGIN          
 INSERT INTO Payment with(rowlock) (BookingId,PaymentType,Amount,PaymentLocation,OfficerId,ReceiptNo,PaymentStatus,EasyPaisaTranNo,IsReferralBookingPaid,ReferralPaymentDate,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy)              
 VALUES(@BookingId,@PaymentType,@Amount,@PaymentLocation,@OfficerId,@ReceiptNo,@PaymentStatus,@EasyPaisaTranNo,@IsReferralBookingPaid,@ReferralPaymentDate,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy)              
 
 select  b.Id as BookingId, b.IsReferralBooking, p.Id, p.PaymentType, p.Pricing, p.Amount, p.PaymentLocation , p.OfficerId, p.ReceiptNo, p.ExtraAmountCharge, p.ExtraAmountReason, p.ExtraAmountReceipt, p.PaymentStatus , p.EasyPaisaTranNo, p.CreatedBy, p.CreatedDate, p.ModifiedBy  , p.ModifiedDate, p.IsReferralBookingPaid , p.ReferralPaymentDate
from Payment p   (nolock)
right join Booking b (nolock) on b.Id =  p.BookingId  
 where P.id=SCOPE_IDENTITY()           
END          
ELSE           
BEGIN          
 UPDATE Payment with(rowlock)
 SET          
 BookingId=@BookingId,          
PaymentType=@PaymentType,          
Amount=@Amount,          
PaymentLocation=@PaymentLocation,          
OfficerId=@OfficerId,          
ReceiptNo=@ReceiptNo,          
PaymentStatus=@PaymentStatus,          
EasyPaisaTranNo=@EasyPaisaTranNo,      
IsReferralBookingPaid = @IsReferralBookingPaid,    
ReferralPaymentDate = @ReferralPaymentDate,      
CreatedBy=@CreatedBy,          
ModifiedBy=@ModifiedBy,    
ModifiedDate=@ModifiedDate          
 WHERE Id=@Id    
       
select  b.Id as BookingId, b.IsReferralBooking,p.Id, p.PaymentType, p.Pricing, p.Amount, p.PaymentLocation , p.OfficerId, p.ReceiptNo, p.ExtraAmountCharge, p.ExtraAmountReason, p.ExtraAmountReceipt, p.PaymentStatus , p.EasyPaisaTranNo, p.CreatedBy, p.CreatedDate, p.ModifiedBy  , p.ModifiedDate, p.IsReferralBookingPaid , p.ReferralPaymentDate
from Payment p (nolock)  
right join Booking b (nolock) on b.Id =  p.BookingId  
 where p.id=@Id          
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveNearestCentreSetup]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveNearestCentreSetup]   
@Id int,  
@CentreId int,  
@NearestCentreId int,  
@NearestLevel int,  
@IsActive bit,  
@CreatedBy int,  
@ModifiedBy int,  
@ModifiedDate datetime  
AS  
BEGIN   
declare @IsExist int

 if @Id is not null and @Id > 0  
	 begin  
	 select @IsExist = ID from NearestCentre nc (nolock) where nc.CentreId = @CentreId and nc.NearestCentreId = @NearestCentreId and nc.Id != @Id
	 if @IsExist is null or @IsExist =0
		 begin
			 update [NearestCentre]  with(rowlock)
			 set   
			 CentreId =  @CentreId,NearestCentreId = @NearestCentreId, NearestLevel = @NearestLevel,IsActive = @IsActive,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate  
			 where id = @Id
			   
			 select nc.Id,ac.Id as CentreId,ac.Name as centreName, ncc.Id NearestCentreId, ncc.Name NearestCentreName, nc.NearestLevel,nc.CreatedBy, nc.CreatedDate, nc.ModifiedBy, nc.ModifiedDate, nc.IsActive
			from NearestCentre nc (nolock)      
			inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on ac.Id=nc.CentreId      
			inner join AlkhidmatCentre ncc (nolock) on ncc.Id =  nc.NearestCentreId 
			 where nc.Id = @Id  
		 end	 	    
	 else
		 begin
			select -1 as Id, @CentreId as CentreId,'' as centreName, @NearestCentreId NearestCentreId, '' NearestCentreName, @NearestLevel NearestLevel,
			@CreatedBy as CreatedBy, GETDATE() CreatedDate, @ModifiedBy ModifiedBy, @ModifiedDate ModifiedDate, @IsActive IsActive
		 end
 end
 else  
	 begin  
	 
	  select @IsExist = ID from NearestCentre nc (nolock) where nc.CentreId = @CentreId and nc.NearestCentreId = @NearestCentreId and nc.Id != @Id
		if @IsExist is null or @IsExist =0
		 begin
			 insert into [NearestCentre]  with(rowlock)
			 (CentreId,NearestCentreId,NearestLevel,IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)  
			 values  
			 (@CentreId,@NearestCentreId,@NearestLevel,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)  

			 select nc.Id,ac.Id as CentreId,ac.Name as centreName, ncc.Id NearestCentreId, ncc.Name NearestCentreName, nc.NearestLevel,
			nc.CreatedBy, nc.CreatedDate, nc.ModifiedBy, nc.ModifiedDate, nc.IsActive
			from NearestCentre nc (nolock)      
			inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on ac.Id=nc.CentreId      
			inner join AlkhidmatCentre ncc (nolock) on ncc.Id =  nc.NearestCentreId  
			where nc.Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()  
		end   
		else
		 begin
			select -1 as Id, @CentreId as CentreId,'' as centreName, @NearestCentreId NearestCentreId, '' NearestCentreName, @NearestLevel NearestLevel,
			@CreatedBy as CreatedBy, GETDATE() CreatedDate, @ModifiedBy ModifiedBy, @ModifiedDate ModifiedDate, @IsActive IsActive
		 end  
	end
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Lookup]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[Lookup]                          
as                          
select Id,[Name] as Description from CauseOfDeath  where IsActive =  1    order by [Name]                    
select Id,[name]  as Description from Town where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]                       
select Id,[name]  as Description,townid from UnionCouncil where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]
select Id,name as Description,UcId from Landmark where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]                        
select Id,name as Description,LandmarkId  from Graveyard where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]                     
select id,vehicleno + ' ( ' +CONVERT(varchar,isnull(AlkhidmatBusNo,0)) + ' )' as Description ,TrackingDeviceId, AlkhidmatBusNo,isnull(IsOnMaintainance,0) as IsOnMaintainance,CentreId from Bus                    
select id,FirstName + ' ' + LastName as Description,Mobile from Driver  order by FirstName + ' ' + LastName
select id,Name as Description from AlkhidmatCentre  where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]                 
select id,(firstName + ' ' + lastname) as Description from [User] where RoleId=3    order by (firstName + ' ' + lastname)                
select Id,Name as Description from PaymentType where IsActive =  1 order by [Name]                                      
select Id,Name as Description from VisitType where IsActive=1  order by [Name]                          
select Id, Name as Description  from [Role]  r where r.IsActive =  1  order by [Name]                                   
select Id, Name as Description  from [RefundType]  r where r.IsActive =  1 order by [Name]
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[RptCentreSummary]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create procedure [dbo].[RptCentreSummary]  
as  
select * from
(
select ac.Id as centreId, ac.Name as centreName,pt.Name as PaymentType, COUNT(b.Id) as BookingCount from AlkhidmatCentre ac
inner join BusVisit bv on ac.Id=bv.CentreId
inner join Booking b on b.Id=bv.BookingId
inner join Payment p on b.Id=p.BookingId
inner join PaymentType pt on pt.Id=p.PaymentType
group by ac.Id,ac.Name,pt.Name
) q
pivot
(
	sum(BookingCount)  for PaymentType in([Cash],[EasyPaisa])
) p
GO

	select l.*, u.Name UcDesc 
	from [Landmark] l (nolock)
inner join UnionCouncil u (nolock) on l.UcId =  u.Id where l.Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()
	end
	
END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveGraveyard] 

@Id	int,
@LandmarkId	int,
@Name	varchar(100),
@IsActive	bit,
@CreatedBy	int,
@ModifiedBy	int,
@ModifiedDate	datetime

AS
BEGIN	
	if @Id is not null and @Id > 0
	begin
	update [Graveyard] with(rowlock)
	set 
	[Name] =  @Name, LandmarkId = @LandmarkId,IsActive = @IsActive,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate
	where id = @Id
	select g.* ,  l.Name LandmarkDesc 
	from [Graveyard] g  (nolock)
inner join Landmark l (nolock) on g.LandmarkId =  l.Id   where g.Id = @Id
	end	
	else
	begin
	insert into Graveyard with(rowlock)
	(LandmarkId,Name,IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)
	values
	(@LandmarkId ,@Name,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)
	
	select g.* ,  l.Name LandmarkDesc 
	from [Graveyard] g (nolock)
inner join Landmark l (nolock) on g.LandmarkId =  l.Id   where g.Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()
	end
	
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveExtraCharges]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveExtraCharges]       
@Id int,      
@BusId int,
@BookingId int,      
@ExtraAmountCharge money,
@ExtraAmountReason nvarchar(500),
@ExtraAmountReceipt nvarchar(50),
@IsActive bit,      
@CreatedBy int,      
@ModifiedBy int,      
@ModifiedDate datetime      
       
AS      
      
BEGIN      
declare @newId int    
 if exists(select id from ExtraCharges (nolock)  where id=@Id and busId=@BusId)   
 begin      
 set @newId=@Id    
 update [ExtraCharges]  with(rowlock)     
 set       
 BusId=@BusId,
 BookingId =  @BookingId,
 ExtraAmountCharge = @ExtraAmountCharge,
 ExtraAmountReason = @ExtraAmountReason,
 ExtraAmountReceipt =@ExtraAmountReceipt,
 IsActive = @IsActive,CreatedBy = @CreatedBy,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate      
 where id = @newId and busId=@BusId     
    
 end       
 else      
 begin      
     
   
 insert into ExtraCharges  with(rowlock)     
 (BusId,BookingId,ExtraAmountCharge,ExtraAmountReason,ExtraAmountReceipt, IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)      
 values      
 (@BusId,@BookingId,@ExtraAmountCharge,@ExtraAmountReason,@ExtraAmountReceipt,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)           
 set @newId=SCOPE_IDENTITY()     
    
 end      
    
 --update Payment set PaymentStatus=2 where BookingId=@BookingId    
 --update BusVisit set IsBookingCompleted=1 where BookingId=@BookingId    

update Payment with(rowlock) set ExtraAmountCharge=(select SUM(ExtraAmountCharge) from ExtraCharges where BookingId=@BookingId)  where BookingId=@BookingId     

 select isnull(ec.Id,0) Id ,ec.BusId,  b.Id as BookingId , isnull(ec.ExtraAmountCharge, 0) ExtraAmountCharge,        
 isnull(ec.ExtraAmountReason,'')as ExtraAmountReason, isnull(ec.ExtraAmountReceipt,'')as ExtraAmountReceipt,       
 ec.IsActive, ec.CreatedBy, ec.CreatedDate,ec.ModifiedBy , ec.ModifiedDate,bv.FuelAmount as BookingAmount  
 from Booking b (nolock)    
 inner join BusVisit bv (nolock) on bv.BookingId=b.Id  
 left join Payment p (nolock)  on b.Id =  p.BookingId      
 left join ExtraCharges ec (nolock) on b.Id = ec.BookingId      
 where ec.Id = @newId      
          
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveDriver] 
@Id	int,
@CentreId	int,
@FirstName	nvarchar(50),
@LastName	nvarchar(50),
@CNIC	nvarchar(13),
@Mobile	nvarchar(13),
@Address	nvarchar(200),
@City	nvarchar(50)= null,
@IsActive	bit,
@CreatedBy	int,
@ModifiedBy	int,
@ModifiedDate DateTime
AS
BEGIN	
	if @Id is not null and @Id > 0
	begin
	update [Driver] with(rowlock)
	set 
	CentreId =  @CentreId,FirstName =  @FirstName,LastName =  @LastName,CNIC = @CNIC,Mobile = @Mobile,[Address] =  @Address,City = @City,IsActive = @IsActive,CreatedBy = @CreatedBy,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy , ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate
	where id = @Id
	select d.* ,  c.Name CentreDesc 
	from [Driver] d (nolock)
	inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=d.centreid where d.Id = @Id
	end	
	else
	begin
	insert into Driver with(rowlock)
	(CentreId,FirstName,LastName,CNIC,Mobile,[Address],City,IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy)
	values
	(@CentreId,@FirstName,@LastName,@CNIC,@Mobile,@Address,@City,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy)
	select d.* ,  c.Name CentreDesc 
	from [Driver] d (nolock)
	inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=d.centreid where d.Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()
	end
	
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveBusVisit]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[SaveBusVisit]                  
@Id int,                  
@CentreId int,                  
@BusId int,                  
@DriverId int,                  
@VisitTypeId int,                  
@BookingId int,                  
@InchargeName nvarchar(30)=null,                
@VisitDate DateTime=null,                
@OutTime tinyint,                
@ReturnTime tinyint,        
@ReturnDate datetime=null,              
@ReadingWhenFilling bigint,                
@PumpLocation nvarchar(50)=null,                
@FuelRate money,                
@FuelAmount money,                
@IsBookingCompleted bit,                  
@InitialReading bigint,                  
@FinalReading bigint,           
@FuelQuantity money,   
@FuelingReceipt nvarchar(50)=null,                
@Description nvarchar(300)=null,  
@BusChangeReason nvarchar(1000)=null,
@IsActive bit,                  
@CreatedBy int,                  
@ModifiedBy int,                  
@ModifiedDate datetime                  
                  
as                  
begin              
declare @newId int      
declare @visitCount int    

--handle special case for editing bus visit info
if @Id is null or @Id=0
begin
  select @Id=id from busvisit (nolock) where busid=@BusId and centreId=@CentreId and BookingId=@BookingId and VisitTypeId=2
end    
    
if @Id is not null and @Id > 0                  
 begin              
 set @newId=@Id                
 update [BusVisit] with(rowlock)                 
 set                   
 CentreId = @CentreId,BusId = @BusId,DriverId = @DriverId,VisitTypeId=  @VisitTypeId,BookingId = @BookingId, InchargeName=@InchargeName,VisitDate=@VisitDate,OutTime=@OutTime,ReturnTime=@ReturnTime,ReturnDate=@ReturnDate,ReadingWhenFilling=@ReadingWhenFilling,  PumpLocation=@PumpLocation,FuelRate=@FuelRate,FuelAmount=@FuelAmount,IsBookingCompleted=@IsBookingCompleted, InitialReading = @InitialReading,FinalReading= @FinalReading,Description=@Description,BusChangeReason=@BusChangeReason,IsActive = @IsActive,CreatedBy = @CreatedBy,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate, FuelQuantity = @FuelQuantity , Receipt = @FuelingReceipt where id = @Id   
 update booking set PickupDate=@VisitDate,PickupTime=@OutTime,ReturnTime=@ReturnTime where Id=@BookingId                
 end                   
 else                  
 begin                  
 select @visitCount=COUNT(id) from BusVisit (nolock) where BusId=@BusId    
 if @visitCount=0     
 begin    
 select @InitialReading= InitialReading from Bus (nolock) where id=@BusId    
 end    
 insert into BusVisit with(rowlock)                 
 (CentreId,BusId,DriverId,VisitTypeId,BookingId,InchargeName,VisitDate,OutTime,ReturnTime,ReturnDate,ReadingWhenFilling,PumpLocation,FuelRate,FuelAmount,IsBookingCompleted,InitialReading,FinalReading,Description,BusChangeReason,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate,FuelQuantity, Receipt)                 
           
 values                  
 (@CentreId,@BusId,@DriverId,@VisitTypeId,@BookingId,@InchargeName,@VisitDate,@OutTime,@ReturnTime,@ReturnDate,@ReadingWhenFilling,@PumpLocation,@FuelRate,@FuelAmount,@IsBookingCompleted,@InitialReading,@FinalReading,@Description,@BusChangeReason,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate,@FuelQuantity, @FuelingReceipt)          
                
 set @newId=SCOPE_IDENTITY()            
 
 update BusVisit with(rowlock) set VisitDate=b.PickupDate,OutTime=b.PickupTime,ReturnTime=b.ReturnTime  from booking b inner join BusVisit bv on bv.BookingId=b.Id  where b.Id=@BookingId                
            
end                  
            
--update BusVisit set FinalReading=@ReadingWhenFilling where id=(select top 1 id from BusVisit where id<>@newId and BusId=@BusId order by VisitDate desc,CreatedDate desc)            
update BusVisit with(rowlock) set BusStatus=3 where id=@newId            
--update BusVisit set VisitDate=b.PickupDate,OutTime=b.PickupTime,ReturnTime=b.ReturnTime from Booking b inner join BusVisit bv on b.Id=bv.BookingId            

        
if @VisitTypeId=3         
begin        
 update Bus with(rowlock) set IsOnMaintainance=1 where id=@BusId        
end        

if @VisitTypeId=3 and @IsBookingCompleted=1         
begin        
 update Bus with(rowlock) set IsOnMaintainance=0 where id=@BusId        
end        
        
select bv.*,t.Name as VisitType ,b.VehicleNo as BusDesc,(d.FirstName + ' ' + d.LastName) as DriverDesc,a.Name as CentreDesc        
from BusVisit bv (nolock)                   
inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId                  
inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=bv.DriverId                  
inner join AlkhidmatCentre a (nolock) on a.Id=bv.CentreId                  
inner join VisitType t (nolock) on t.Id=bv.VisitTypeId  where bv.Id = @newId             
            
end
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveBus]         
@Id int,        
@CentreId int,          
@VehicleNo varchar(50),          
@AlkhidmatBusNo int,      
@TrackingDeviceId varchar(50)=null,        
@ModelNo varchar(50),        
@No varchar(50)=null,        
@InitialReading bigint,  
@Description nvarchar(200)=null,        
@IsActive bit,        
@CreatedBy int,        
@ModifiedBy int,        
@ModifiedDate datetime        
        
AS        
BEGIN         
 if @Id is not null and @Id > 0        
 begin        
 update [Bus]  with(rowlock)      
 set         
 CentreId = @CentreId,TrackingDeviceId = @TrackingDeviceId,VehicleNo  = @VehicleNo,ModelNo = @ModelNo, [No] =  @No,InitialReading=@InitialReading, [Description]= @Description,IsActive = @IsActive,CreatedBy = @CreatedBy,ModifiedBy = @ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate = @ModifiedDate, AlkhidmatBusNo = @AlkhidmatBusNo        
 where id = @Id     
        
 select b.*,c.name as CentreDesc 
 from [Bus] b (nolock)    
 inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=b.centreid    
  where b.Id = @Id        
 end         
 else        
 begin        
 insert into Bus with(rowlock)       
 (CentreId,TrackingDeviceId,VehicleNo ,ModelNo, [No],InitialReading,[Description],IsActive,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate, AlkhidmatBusNo)        
 values        
 (@CentreId,@TrackingDeviceId,@VehicleNo,@ModelNo, @No,@InitialReading,@Description,@IsActive,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate,@AlkhidmatBusNo)        
     
 select b.*,c.name as CentreDesc 
 from [Bus] b (nolock)     
 inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.id=b.centreid    
  where b.Id = SCOPE_IDENTITY()        
 end        
         
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveBooking]            
@Id int=null,        
@ContactName nvarchar(100),      
@ContactMobile nvarchar(100),      
@ContactNic nvarchar(100)=null,      
@DeseasedName nvarchar(100)=null,      
@DeseasedAge smallint=null,      
@DeseasedGender smallint=null,      
@CauseOfDeath smallint=null,      
@Address varchar(50)=null,      
@BusPoint int =null,      
@LandmarkId int =null,      
@UnionCouncilId int =null,      
@TownId int =null,      
@PickupDate datetime =null,      
@PickupTime smallint =null,      
@ReturnTime smallint =null,      
@GraveyardId smallint=null,      
@NamazEJanazaHeldIn smallint=null,       
@NamazEJanazaLocation nvarchar(100)=null,      
@MasjidName nvarchar(100)=null,
@IsReferralBooking bit = null,
@ReferralName nvarchar(100)=  null,
@ReferralDetail nvarchar(400)= null,
@OtherDetail nvarchar(400)=null,  
@alkhidmatCentre int,
@CreatedBy int,  
@ModifiedBy int,  
@ModifiedDate datetime,  
@IsActive bit=1      
as            
 
declare @newId int
IF @Id=null or @Id=0        
BEGIN        
 INSERT INTO Booking with(rowlock)(ContactName,ContactMobile,ContactNic,DeseasedName,DeseasedAge,DeseasedGender,CauseOfDeath,Address,BusPoint,LandmarkId,UnionCouncilId,TownId,PickupDate,PickupTime,ReturnTime,GraveyardId,NamazEJanazaHeldIn,NamazEJanazaLocation,MasjidName,IsReferralBooking,ReferralName, ReferralDetail, OtherDetail,alkhidmatCentre,CreatedBy,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate)                  
 VALUES(@ContactName,@ContactMobile,@ContactNic,@DeseasedName,@DeseasedAge,@DeseasedGender,@CauseOfDeath,@Address,@BusPoint,@LandmarkId,@UnionCouncilId,@TownId,@PickupDate,@PickupTime,@ReturnTime,@GraveyardId,@NamazEJanazaHeldIn,@NamazEJanazaLocation,@MasjidName,@IsReferralBooking, @ReferralName, @ReferralDetail, @OtherDetail,@alkhidmatCentre,@CreatedBy,@ModifiedBy,@ModifiedDate)            
 set @newId=SCOPE_IDENTITY()
 
END        
ELSE         
BEGIN        
 UPDATE Booking with (rowlock) SET        
 ContactName = @ContactName,        
 ContactMobile=@ContactMobile,        
 ContactNic=@ContactNic,        
 DeseasedName=@DeseasedName,        
 DeseasedAge=@DeseasedAge,        
 DeseasedGender=@DeseasedGender,        
 CauseOfDeath=@CauseOfDeath,        
 Address=@Address,        
 BusPoint=@BusPoint,        
 LandmarkId=@LandmarkId,        
 UnionCouncilId=@UnionCouncilId,        
 TownId=@TownId,        
 PickupDate=@PickupDate,    
 PickupTime=@PickupTime,        
 ReturnTime=@ReturnTime,        
 GraveyardId=@GraveyardId,        
 NamazEJanazaHeldIn=@NamazEJanazaHeldIn,      
NamazEJanazaLocation=@NamazEJanazaLocation,      
MasjidName=@MasjidName,    
IsReferralBooking= @IsReferralBooking,
ReferralName =  @ReferralName,
ReferralDetail  = @ReferralDetail,  
OtherDetail=@OtherDetail,  
alkhidmatCentre = @alkhidmatCentre,
ModifiedBy=@ModifiedBy,  
ModifiedDate=@ModifiedDate  
 WHERE Id=@Id        
 set @newId=@Id
 update BusVisit with (rowlock) set VisitDate=@PickupDate,OutTime=@PickupTime,ReturnTime=@ReturnTime where BookingId=@Id
 --from Booking b inner join BusVisit bv on b.Id=bv.BookingId            
 
 
END
--select Id,ContactName,ContactMobile,ContactNic,DeseasedName,DeseasedAge,DeseasedGender,CauseOfDeath,Address,BusPoint,LandmarkId,UnionCouncilId,TownId,PickupDate,PickupTime,ReturnTime,GraveyardId,NamazEJanazaHeldIn,NamazEJanazaLocation,MasjidName,OtherDetail,IsActive,CreatedBy,CreatedDate,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate,IsReferralBooking,ReferralName,ReferralDetail,alkhidmatCentre from Booking(nolock) where id=@newId         
select @newId as id
--,CreatedBy,CreatedDate,ModifiedBy,ModifiedDate from Booking(nolock) where id=@newId
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[ResetUserPassword]
@UserId int,
@Password nvarchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	update [User] set [Password] = @Password where id =  @UserId
	
	if @@ROWCOUNT <=0
	begin
		RAISERROR ('User Password has not been reset successfully.', -- Message text.  
         16, -- Severity.  
         1 -- State.   
         );  
	end
END

CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetPaymentById]    
@Id int    
AS    
select  b.Id as BookingId, b.IsReferralBooking,p.Id, p.PaymentType, p.Pricing, p.Amount, p.PaymentLocation , p.OfficerId, p.ReceiptNo, p.ExtraAmountCharge, p.ExtraAmountReason, p.ExtraAmountReceipt, p.PaymentStatus , p.EasyPaisaTranNo, p.CreatedBy, p.CreatedDate, p.ModifiedBy  , p.ModifiedDate, p.IsReferralBookingPaid , p.ReferralPaymentDate
from Payment p(nolock)   
right join Booking b(nolock) on b.Id =  p.BookingId  
where b.id=@id

CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetNearestCentreSetupById]       
@Id int          
as          
begin          
select nc.Id,ac.Id as CentreId,ac.Name as centreName, ncc.Id NearestCentreId, ncc.Name NearestCentreName, nc.NearestLevel,
nc.CreatedBy, nc.CreatedDate, nc.ModifiedBy, nc.ModifiedDate, nc.IsActive
from NearestCentre nc (nolock)        
inner join AlkhidmatCentre ac (nolock) on ac.Id=nc.CentreId        
inner join AlkhidmatCentre ncc (nolock) on ncc.Id =  nc.NearestCentreId  
where nc.Id=@Id       
order by ac.Name, nc.NearestLevel       
end

CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetBusVisitByCriteria]    
@BookingId int   
as    
begin    
select b.*,vt.Name as VisitType,bus.VehicleNo as busDesc,(d.FirstName + ',' + d.LastName) as driverDesc,c.Name as centreDesc  
from [BusVisit] b(nolock)   
inner join Bus (nolock)on bus.Id=b.BusId  
inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=b.DriverId  
inner join AlkhidmatCentre c(nolock) on c.Id=b.CentreId  
inner join VisitType vt (nolock) on b.VisitTypeId=vt.Id
where b.BookingId=@BookingId and b.IsActive=1     
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[RptBusDetailReport]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- [dbo].[RptBusDetailReport]       @busid=  1  
   
CREATE procedure [dbo].[RptBusDetailReport] 
@FromBookingDate datetime =  null,
@ToBookingDate datetime =  null,          
 @BusId int   
 as  
 begin  
  
select  asv.VehicleNo, asv.VisitDate, asv.VisitType, asv.FuelAmount Amount , asv.FinalReading, asv.InitialReading, asv.milage   
, asv.outTime ,  asv.returnTime,  asv.visitInterval, asv.driver, asv.centre   
from AdminSummary_View asv (nolock) where asv.BusId=@BusId 
and  DATEDIFF(day, @FromBookingDate, asv.VisitDate) >= 0 and DATEDIFF(day , asv.VisitDate, @ToBookingDate) >= 0  
--and asv.VisitTypeId <> 1   
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetNearestCentreById]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetNearestCentreById]      
@Id int      
as      
begin      
select nc.Id,c.Id as centreId,c.Name as centreName, dbo.GetCsvBuses(c.Id) busList,c.Address,c.ContactNo1,c.ContactNo2,    
nc.CreatedBy,nc.ModifiedBy,nc.IsActive,nc.CreatedDate,nc.ModifiedDate,nc.NearestLevel     
from NearestCentre nc  (nolock)   
inner join AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) on c.Id=nc.NearestCentreId    
where nc.CentreId=@Id   
  
--union   
--select c.Id,c.Id as centreId,c.Name as centreName, dbo.GetCsvBuses(c.Id) busList,c.Address,c.ContactNo1,c.ContactNo2,    
--nc.CreatedBy,nc.ModifiedBy,nc.IsActive,nc.CreatedDate,nc.ModifiedDate,0 as NearestLevel     
--from NearestCentre nc     
--inner join AlkhidmatCentre c on c.Id=nc.NearestCentreId    
--where c.Id=@Id 

union   
select c.Id,c.Id as centreId,c.Name as centreName, dbo.GetCsvBuses(c.Id) busList,c.Address,c.ContactNo1,c.ContactNo2,    
c.CreatedBy,c.ModifiedBy,c.IsActive,c.CreatedDate,c.ModifiedDate,0 as NearestLevel     
from AlkhidmatCentre c (nolock) where c.Id=@Id 


order by NearestLevel   
  
end

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[RptDriverSummary]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[RptDriverSummary]
as
select driverId,Driver as DriverName,CONVERT(varchar,SUM(milage)) + ' km' as milage,COUNT(BusVisitId) as visitCount from AdminSummary_View
group by driverId,Driver
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[rptDashboardBookingSummary]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[rptDashboardBookingSummary]
@FromBookingDate datetime =  null,
@ToBookingDate datetime =  null,
@CentreId int =  null
as
begin
select top 5 cte.CentreId, cte.Centre, SUM(cte.BookingAmount) BookingAmount, 
SUM(cte.BookingMilage) BookingMilage, SUM(cte.Bookings) Bookings, SUM(cte.Receivable) Receivable,SUM(cte.Maintenance) Maintenance, 
(SUM(cte.BookingAmount) - SUM(cte.Maintenance)) as Profit

from (
select asv.CentreId, asv.centre,asv.VisitTypeId, 
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and (isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 0 or ( isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) = 1) )  then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end BookingAmount,   
--case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) else 0 end BookingMilage,    
SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) BookingMilage,    
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then COUNT(isnull(asv.BookingId,0)) else 0 end Bookings,
case when asv.VisitTypeId = 1 or  asv.VisitTypeId = 3 OR asv.VisitTypeId = 4 then sum(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Maintenance,    
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) <> 1 then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Receivable
from AdminSummary_View asv 
--where asv.VisitTypeId <> 1
group by asv.CentreId, asv.centre, asv.VisitTypeId,isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0),ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) 
) cte
group by cte.centre, cte.CentreId
order by BookingAmount desc, Bookings desc
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[rptCentreReport]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[rptCentreReport]    
@FromBookingDate datetime =  null,    
@ToBookingDate datetime =  null,    
@CentreId int =  null    
as    
begin    
select cte.CentreId, cte.Centre, SUM(cte.BookingAmount) BookingAmount,     
SUM(cte.BookingMilage) BookingMilage, SUM(cte.Bookings) Bookings, SUM(cte.Receivable) Receivable,SUM(cte.Maintenance) Maintenance,     
(SUM(cte.BookingAmount) - SUM(cte.Maintenance)) as Profit    
    
from (    
select asv.CentreId, asv.centre,asv.VisitTypeId,     
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and (isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 0 or ( isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) = 1) )  then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end BookingAmount,     
--case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) else 0 end BookingMilage,    
SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) BookingMilage,    
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then COUNT(isnull(asv.BookingId,0)) else 0 end Bookings,    
case when asv.VisitTypeId = 1 or  asv.VisitTypeId = 3 OR asv.VisitTypeId = 4 then sum(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Maintenance,    
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) <> 1 then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Receivable    
from AdminSummary_View asv  (nolock)   
--where asv.VisitTypeId <> 1    
where DATEDIFF(day, @FromBookingDate, asv.VisitDate) >= 0 and DATEDIFF(day , asv.VisitDate, @ToBookingDate) >= 0  
group by asv.CentreId, asv.centre, asv.VisitTypeId,isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0),ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0)     
) cte    
group by cte.centre, cte.CentreId    
order by BookingAmount desc, Bookings desc
    
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[rptBusWiseCentreReport]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[rptBusWiseCentreReport]  
@FromBookingDate datetime =  null,  
@ToBookingDate datetime =  null,  
@CentreId int  
as  
begin  
  
select cte.CentreId, cte.Centre, cte.VehicleNo, cte.BusId, SUM(cte.BookingAmount) BookingAmount,   
SUM(cte.BookingMilage) BookingMilage, SUM(cte.Maintenance) Maintenance, SUM(cte.Bookings) Bookings, SUM(cte.Receivable) Receivable  
from (  
select asv.CentreId, asv.centre, asv.VehicleNo, asv.BusId,  
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and (isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 0 or ( isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) = 1) )  then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end BookingAmount,   
--case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) else 0 end BookingMilage,    
SUM(isnull(asv.milage,0)) BookingMilage,     
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 then COUNT(isnull(asv.BookingId,0)) else 0 end Bookings,  
case when asv.VisitTypeId = 1 or  asv.VisitTypeId = 3 OR asv.VisitTypeId = 4 then sum(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Maintenance,  
case when asv.VisitTypeId =2 and isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0) = 1 and ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0) <> 1 then SUM(isnull(asv.FuelAmount,0)) else 0 end Receivable  
from AdminSummary_View asv  (nolock) 
where  asv.CentreId=@CentreId 
and DATEDIFF(day, @FromBookingDate, asv.VisitDate) >= 0 and DATEDIFF(day , asv.VisitDate, @ToBookingDate) >= 0  --and asv.VisitTypeId <> 1  
group by asv.CentreId, asv.centre, asv.VehicleNo, asv.BusId,  asv.VisitTypeId,isnull(asv.IsReferralBooking,0),ISNULL(asv.IsReferralBookingPaid ,0)  
) cte  
group by cte.centre, cte.CentreId, cte.VehicleNo, cte.BusId  
  
end
GO

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_audit_RefundBooking]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_audit_RefundBooking](              
    @seqval as binary(10),        
    @flag as smallint        
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)          
AS          
BEGIN          
declare @result varchar(max)              
        
select top 1 @result=         
case @flag         
when 1 then convert(varchar,b.BookingId)         
when 2 then convert(varchar,b.ActualBookingAmount)        
when 3 then [dbo].[fn_GetTown](convert(varchar,b.RefundOfficeLocation) )       
when 4 then [dbo].[fn_GetRefundType](b.RefundTypeId)       
when 5 then CONVERT(varchar, b.RefundAmount)        
when 6 then CONVERT(varchar, b.RefundReason)        
when 7 then CONVERT(varchar, b.RefundReceipt)        
when 8 then [dbo].[fn_GetOfficer](CONVERT(varchar, b.RefundOfficer))        
when 9 then [dbo].[fn_GetBus](b.BusId)        
--when 9 then CONVERT(varchar, b.IsActive)        
--when 10 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedBy)        
--when 11 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedDate)        
--when 12 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedBy)        
--when 13 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedDate)        
else ''        
end        
from cdc.dbo_RefundBooking_Ct b where b.__$operation in(2,3) and  b.__$seqval=@seqval        
return @result           
end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_audit_payment]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_audit_payment](              
    @seqval as binary(10),        
    @flag as smallint        
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)          
AS          
BEGIN          
declare @result varchar(max)              
        
select top 1 @result=         
case @flag         
when 1 then convert(varchar,b.BookingId)         
when 2 then [dbo].[fn_GetPaymantType](convert(varchar,b.PaymentType) )       
when 3 then convert(varchar,b.Pricing)        
when 4 then CONVERT(varchar, b.Amount)        
when 5 then [dbo].[fn_GetTown](CONVERT(varchar, b.PaymentLocation) )       
when 6 then [dbo].[fn_GetOfficer](CONVERT(varchar, b.OfficerId))        
when 7 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReceiptNo)        
when 8 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ExtraAmountCharge)        
when 9 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ExtraAmountReason)        
when 10 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ExtraAmountReceipt)        
when 11 then [dbo].[fn_PaymentStatus](CONVERT(varchar, b.PaymentStatus))        
when 12 then CONVERT(varchar, b.EasyPaisaTranNo)        
when 13 then dbo.fn_GetBoolean(b.IsReferralBookingPaid)        
when 14 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReferralPaymentDate)        

--when 13 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedBy)        
--when 14 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedDate)        
--when 15 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedBy)        
--when 16 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedDate)        
else ''        
end        
from cdc.dbo_payment_Ct b where b.__$operation in(2,3) and  b.__$seqval=@seqval        
return @result           
end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_audit_BusVisit]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_audit_BusVisit](                  
    @seqval as binary(10),            
    @flag as smallint            
    )              
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)              
AS              
BEGIN              
declare @result varchar(max)                  
            
select top 1 @result=             
case @flag             
when 1 then [dbo].[fn_GetCentre](b.CentreId)             
when 2 then [dbo].[fn_GetBus](b.BusId)    
when 3 then [dbo].[fn_GetDriver](b.DriverId)       
when 4 then [dbo].[fn_GetVisitType](b.VisitTypeId)            
--when 5 then CONVERT(varchar, b.BookingId)            
when 6 then CONVERT(varchar, b.InchargeName)            
when 7 then CONVERT(varchar, b.VisitDate)            
when 8 then [dbo].[fn_GetTimeSlot](b.OutTime)           
when 9 then [dbo].[fn_GetTimeSlot]( b.ReturnTime)            
when 10 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReturnDate)            
when 11 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReadingWhenFilling)            
when 12 then CONVERT(varchar, b.PumpLocation)            
when 13 then CONVERT(varchar, b.FuelRate)            
when 14 then CONVERT(varchar, b.FuelAmount)            
when 15 then CONVERT(varchar, b.Receipt)            
when 16 then [dbo].[fn_GetBoolean](b.IsBookingCompleted)            
when 17 then CONVERT(varchar, b.InitialReading)            
when 18 then CONVERT(varchar, b.FinalReading)            
when 19 then CONVERT(varchar, b.Description)            
when 20 then dbo.GetBusStatus(b.BusStatus)            
when 21 then CONVERT(varchar, b.FuelQuantity)             
when 22 then CONVERT(varchar, b.BusChangeReason)             
--when 22 then CONVERT(varchar, b.IsActive)            
--when 23 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedBy)            
--when 24 then CONVERT(varchar, b.CreatedDate)            
--when 25 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedBy)            
--when 26 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedDate)            
else ''            
end            
from cdc.dbo_BusVisit_Ct b where b.__$operation in(2,3) and  b.__$seqval=@seqval            
return @result               
end
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_audit_booking]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_audit_booking](                  
    @seqval as binary(10),            
    @flag as smallint            
    )              
RETURNS VARCHAR(20)              
AS              
BEGIN              
declare @result varchar(max)                  
            
select top 1 @result=             
case @flag             
when 1 then isnull(b.contactName,'')             
when 2 then isnull(b.ContactMobile,'')            
when 3 then isnull(b.ContactNic,'')            
when 4 then CONVERT(varchar, b.DeseasedName)            
when 5 then CONVERT(varchar, b.DeseasedAge)            
when 6 then dbo.fn_GetGender(b.DeseasedGender)            
when 7 then dbo.fn_GetCauseOfDeath(CONVERT(varchar, b.CauseOfDeath))            
when 8 then CONVERT(varchar, b.Address)            
when 9 then dbo.fn_GetLandmark(b.BusPoint)            
when 10 then dbo.fn_GetLandmark(b.LandmarkId)            
when 11 then dbo.fn_GetUnionCouncil(b.UnionCouncilId)            
when 12 then dbo.fn_GetTown(b.TownId)            
when 13 then CONVERT(varchar, b.PickupDate)            
when 14 then dbo.[fn_GetTimeSlot](CONVERT(varchar, b.PickupTime))            
when 15 then dbo.[fn_GetTimeSlot](CONVERT(varchar, b.ReturnTime))            
when 16 then dbo.[fn_GetGraveyard](CONVERT(varchar, b.GraveyardId))            
when 17 then dbo.[fn_GetParyer]( CONVERT(varchar, b.NamazEJanazaHeldIn))            
when 18 then CONVERT(varchar, b.NamazEJanazaLocation)            
when 19 then CONVERT(varchar, b.MasjidName)            
when 20 then CONVERT(varchar, b.OtherDetail)            

when 21 then dbo.fn_GetBoolean(b.IsReferralBooking)            
when 22 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReferralName)            
when 23 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ReferralDetail)            
when 24 then dbo.fn_GetCentre(b.alkhidmatCentre)            

--when 21 then CONVERT(varchar, b.IsActive)            
--when 22 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedBy)            
--when 23 then CONVERT(varchar, b.ModifiedDate)            
else ''            
end            
from cdc.dbo_booking_Ct b where b.__$operation in(2,3) and  b.__$seqval=@seqval            
return @result               
end
GO

CREATE  FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetNextBusVisitId](                  
    @BusId as int,
    @CurrentId int  
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(500)          
AS          
begin  
declare @result int              
  
  SELECT @result = MIN(asv.busvisitid) 
  FROM AdminSummary_View asv (nolock)
WHERE asv.busvisitid > @CurrentId and asv.VisitTypeId = 1 and asv.BusId = @BusId
  
--select @result = u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName  from [User] u where id = @Id
return @result   
end
GO

CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetPreviousBusVisitId](                  
    @BusId as int,
    @CurrentId int  
    )          
RETURNS VARCHAR(500)          
AS          
begin  
declare @result int              
  
  SELECT @result = Max(asv.busvisitid) 
  FROM AdminSummary_View asv (nolock)
WHERE asv.busvisitid < @CurrentId and asv.VisitTypeId = 1 and asv.BusId = @BusId
  
--select @result = u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName  from [User] u where id = @Id

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_GetPreviousBusMeterReading]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetPreviousBusMeterReading](                  
    @BusId as int,
    @CurrentId int  
    )          
RETURNS bigint
AS          
begin  
declare @result bigint
declare @visitCount int
select @visitCount=COUNT(id) from BusVisit (nolock) where BusId=@BusId
 if @visitCount=0 
 begin
	select @result= InitialReading from Bus (nolock) where id=@BusId
 end
 else
 begin  
	SELECT @result = isnull(Max(asv.FinalReading),0) 
	FROM AdminSummary_View asv (nolock)
	WHERE asv.busvisitid < @CurrentId and asv.BusId = @BusId
	
	if @result=0
	begin
		select @result= InitialReading from Bus (nolock) where id=@BusId
	end
end
  
--select @result = u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName  from [User] u where id = @Id
return @result   
end
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetBookingStatstics]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE  procedure [dbo].[GetBookingStatstics] 
@OfficerId int
as

declare @TodaysBooking int, @UserPiadBooking int, @UserUnpaidBooking int,@UserCancelBooking int
begin
select @TodaysBooking = isnull(COUNT(*),0) from CCTracking_View cctv where LEFT(CONVERT(VARCHAR, cctv.PickupDate, 120), 10) =  LEFT(CONVERT(VARCHAR, GETDATE(), 120), 10)
select @UserPiadBooking =  isnull(COUNT(*),0) FROM CCTracking_View cctv where cctv.BookingUser =  @OfficerId and cctv.PaymentStatus = 1
select @UserUnpaidBooking =  isnull(COUNT(*),0) FROM CCTracking_View cctv where cctv.BookingUser =  @OfficerId and isnull(cctv.PaymentStatus,0) = 0
select @UserCancelBooking =  isnull(COUNT(*),0) FROM CCTracking_View cctv where cctv.BookingUser =  @OfficerId and isnull(cctv.PaymentStatus,0) = 2
 
 
 select @TodaysBooking TodaysBooking, @UserPiadBooking + @UserUnpaidBooking + @UserCancelBooking as UserTotalBooking, @UserPiadBooking UserPiadBooking, @UserUnpaidBooking UserUnpaidBooking
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetBusVisitById]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetBusVisitById]       
@Id int        
as        
begin        
select bv.Id,bv.CentreId,bv.BusId,bv.DriverId,bv.VisitTypeId,bv.BookingId,bv.InchargeName,bv.VisitDate,bv.OutTime,bv.ReturnTime,bv.ReturnDate,    
bv.ReadingWhenFilling,bv.PumpLocation,bv.FuelRate,bv.FuelAmount,bv.IsBookingCompleted,    
dbo.fn_GetPreviousBusMeterReading(bv.BusId,bv.Id) as InitialReading,    
bv.FinalReading    
,bv.Description,  
bv.BusChangeReason,  
bv.BusStatus,bv.IsActive,bv.CreatedBy,bv.CreatedDate,bv.ModifiedBy,bv.ModifiedDate,bv.FuelQuantity,  bv.Receipt,  
t.Name as VisitType ,b.VehicleNo as BusDesc,(d.FirstName + ' ' + d.LastName) as DriverDesc,a.Name as CentreDesc           
from BusVisit bv  (nolock)        
inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId        
inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=bv.DriverId        
inner join AlkhidmatCentre a (nolock) on a.Id=bv.CentreId        
left join VisitType t (nolock) on t.Id=bv.VisitTypeId        
where bv.IsActive=1 and bv.Id=@Id        
      
end
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetAllBusVisit]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[GetAllBusVisit]      
@Id int      
as        
select bv.Id,b.VehicleNo as BusDesc,bv.BookingId,t.Name as VisitType, bv.VisitDate,bv.ReturnDate,bv.FinalReading,dbo.fn_GetPreviousBusMeterReading(bv.BusId,bv.Id) InitialReading

--,bv.CentreId,bv.BusId,bv.DriverId,bv.VisitTypeId,bv.InchargeName,bv.OutTime,bv.ReturnTime,
--bv.ReadingWhenFilling,bv.PumpLocation,bv.FuelRate,bv.FuelAmount,bv.IsBookingCompleted,    
    

--,bv.Description,bv.BusChangeReason,    
--bv.BusStatus,bv.IsActive,bv.CreatedBy,bv.CreatedDate,bv.ModifiedBy,bv.ModifiedDate,bv.FuelQuantity, bv.Receipt,   

--,(d.FirstName + ' ' + d.LastName) as DriverDesc,a.Name as CentreDesc         
from BusVisit bv  (nolock)     
inner join Bus b (nolock) on b.Id=bv.BusId and bv.busId=@Id         
--inner join Driver d (nolock) on d.Id=bv.DriverId      
--inner join AlkhidmatCentre a (nolock) on a.Id=bv.CentreId      
left join VisitType t (nolock) on t.Id=bv.VisitTypeId      
where bv.IsActive=1 
order by bv.Id desc
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_GetPreviousBusFuelingReading]    Script Date: 02/21/2015 01:17:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_GetPreviousBusFuelingReading](                  
    @BusId as int,
    @CurrentId int  
    )          
RETURNS bigint
AS          
begin  
declare @result bigint ,  @PreviousBusVisitId int            
  
  select @PreviousBusVisitId  =  dbo.fn_GetPreviousBusVisitId(@BusId, @CurrentId)
  
  SELECT @result = bv.ReadingWhenFilling from BusVisit bv where bv.Id = @PreviousBusVisitId
  
  
--select @result = u.FirstName + ' ' + u.LastName  from [User] u where id = @Id
return @result   
end
